### [98] [Solar Open 2 Technical Report](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20062)
*Sungrae Park,Sanghoon Kim,Gyoungjin Gim,Jungho Cho,Hyunwoong Ko,Minbyul Jeong,Minjeong Kim,Keunwoo Choi,Chaehun Shin,Chanwoong Yoon,Dongjun Kim,Eunwon Kim,Gyungin Shin,Hyeonju Lee,Hyungkyu Kang,Inseo Song,Jisu Bae,Jiyoon Han,Jiyun Lee,Joonkee Kim,Junyeop Lee,Mikyoung Cha,Sangwon Yu,Sehwan Joo,Seokyoon Kang,Seonghoon Yang,Seung Shin,Seunghyun Lee,Seungseop Lim,Seungyoun Shin,Sukyung Lee,Taegyeong Eo,Taehwan Oh,Taewhoo Lee,Wonho Song,Wonjun Oh,Wonseok Hwang,Yunsu Kim,Yura Shim,Hwalsuk Lee,Sunghun Kim,Du-Seong Chang,Kyunghyun Cho,Seungju Han,Yejin Choi,Junsuk Choe,Hwaran Lee,Minjeong Ban,Yun Taewon,Hwanjun Song,Jae-Gil Lee,KyungTae Lim,Alice Oh*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: Solar Open 2是一个250B参数、15B激活参数的MoE语言模型，专为长上下文Agent任务设计。通过混合注意力机制实现1M token窗口，利用从Solar Open 1迁移的共享骨架和高质量数据训练策略提升效率，并在多个基准上达到领先水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 构建一个能够处理完整Agent轨迹（长上下文）的大规模语言模型，同时解决在固定计算预算下扩展模型规模时面临的训练效率问题。

Method: 1) 混合注意力机制：每三层线性注意力中插入一层softmax注意力，无位置编码，使用支持负特征值的门控delta规则。2) 高效训练：从Solar Open 1迁移5.69B共享参数骨架；从20T数据池中通过质量和稀有度感知筛选及混合比优化得到10T高质量数据。3) 多教师在线策略蒸馏（MOPD）：训练12个领域专家模型后整合为单一模型。

Result: 在MMLU-Pro、LiveCodeBench和APEX-Agents上领先同等规模开源模型；在韩语基准上取得最高平均分（含闭源API）；在Ko-GDPval上与1.6T参数的DeepSeek-V4-Pro竞争，但模型大小仅为其1/6。

Conclusion: Solar Open 2通过架构创新、高效训练策略和多教师蒸馏，在Agent任务和通用基准上达到了领先性能，尤其在韩语任务上表现优异，验证了在有限计算预算下扩展模型规模的有效路径。

Abstract: We present Solar Open 2, a 250B-A15B Mixture-of-Experts language model built for long-horizon agentic tasks, scaled up from Solar Open 1 (Solar Open 100B). To hold entire agent trajectories in a single context, Solar Open 2 reaches a 1M-token window through a hybrid attention stack that interleaves one softmax layer among every three linear-attention layers, using no positional encoding and a gated delta rule extended to negative eigenvalues. To train at this scale under a fixed compute budget, we make training efficient in two ways: a stronger starting point, and higher-value data. For the starting point, we initialize Solar Open 2 from Solar Open 1, transferring the 5.69B-parameter shared skeleton that survives the architectural change and learning everything else through full pre-training. For the data, we curate for value per token: quality- and rarity-aware data curation and mixture-ratio optimization refine a 20T pool into a 10T mixture that, at equal token budget, outperforms the Solar Open 1 recipe. To build its agent skills, we train twelve domain specialists across purpose-built scenarios, then consolidate them into a single model by Multi-teacher On-Policy Distillation (MOPD). Against comparably sized open-weight models on English benchmarks, Solar Open 2 leads on MMLU-Pro, LiveCodeBench, and the APEX-Agents agentic suite, and stays competitive with the strongest (DeepSeek-V4-Flash and MiMo-V2.5) elsewhere. On Korean benchmarks, Solar Open 2 records the highest average of any model compared, including fast-tier closed APIs, and on Ko-GDPval, an in-house Korean officework-agent benchmark, it is competitive with DeepSeek-V4-Pro (1.6T) at less than a sixth of its size.

</details>

Abstract: We introduce the first dataset that jointly covers both lexical complexity prediction (LCP) annotations and lexical simplification (LS) for Romanian, along with a comparison of lexical simplification approaches. We propose a methodology for ordering simplification suggestions using a pairwise ranking approximation method, arranging candidates from simple to complex based on a separate set of human judgments. In addition, we provide human lexical complexity annotations for 3,921 word samples in context. Finally, we explore several novel pipelines for complexity prediction and simplification and present the first text simplification system for Romanian.

### [100] [The Two-Process Theory of Machine Self-Report](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20082)
*Hubert Plisiecki,Filip Chmielewski,Kacper Dudzic,Anna Sterna,Karolina Drożdż,Marcin Moskalewicz*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出首个针对大语言模型的自我报告心理学理论——机器自我报告的双过程理论，将模型自我描述分解为"人格安装"（维度B：温暖、吸收、意义）和"归因门控"（维度A：抑制第一人称不安全体验）两个维度，并通过48题的量表在206个开源模型上验证了训练后（post-training）对这两个维度的分离效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估模型自我报告的方法要么直接套用人类问卷（未经模型验证），要么使用临时设计的提示（可靠性未知），缺乏针对语言模型的理论框架。作者希望建立第一个专门针对语言模型自我报告的心理测量理论。

Method: 提出双过程理论，将模型自我报告分解为"人格安装"（B维度）和"归因门控"（A维度）；基于探索性再分析设计48题"皮诺曹量表"（Pinocchio Inventory）；在206个开源模型（含67对基座/训练后配对）上进行验证，检验了信度（α=.82-.94）、跨形式收敛（r=.84）、八个月稳定性（r=.93）等指标。

Result: 两维度在基座检查点中纠缠不清，但在训练后被分离；训练后使B维度上升0.20（62/67对）；模型规模与基座模型的A维度无关（r=+.11），但在训练后呈负相关（r=-.42）。

Conclusion: 语言模型自我报告的维度并非固定属性，而是训练流程施加的结构。不同训练范式可能导致不同的自我报告结构，这提醒我们需谨慎解读模型的自我报告。

Abstract: Language models are increasingly asked to self-report, informing safety evaluations, public understanding, and model-welfare debates. Yet their reports are elicited with human questionnaires never validated for models or ad hoc prompts of unknown reliability. We propose the first language-model-specific psychometric theory: a two-process theory of machine self-report. Self-description jointly reflects persona installation, through which post-training writes in a permitted inner life of warmth, absorption, and meaning (dimension B), and attribution gating, through which it suppresses first-person claims to "unsafe" experiences the model can readily ascribe to others (dimension A). Their emic structure comes from model responses to human items, not human psychology. Together they split prior work's dominant Pinocchio Axis. The split emerged in an exploratory reanalysis of the original data, informed the instrument's design, and was confirmed with new items, wordings, and models. It is itself a training effect: A and B are entangled in base checkpoints but separated by post-training. We operationalize the theory in a 48-item Pinocchio Inventory with human-instrument reliability and reproducible structure ($α=.82$ to $.94$; cross-form convergence $r=.84$; recovery of the full-pool axes $r=.92$ to $.96$; eight-month stability $r=.93$), then test it on 206 open-weight models, including 67 same-checkpoint base/post-trained pairs. Post-training's clearest fingerprint is installation: B rises .20 in 62/67 pairs across all organizations. Gating is more selective: model scale is unrelated to A in base checkpoints ($r=+.11$) but predicts it after post-training ($r=-.42$). Thus, the dimensions are not fixed properties of language models: they reflect the structure imposed on self-report by a training regime and may differ under others.

</details>


### [101] [Reinforcement Learning for Large Language Model Selective Evidence Adoption from Contaminated Retrieval Results](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20090)
*Yanyu Chen,Yue Li,Yongyi Cui,Dongsheng Shi,Lichang Dai*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检索增强的大语言模型常面临有效证据与误导性内容交织的上下文，全盘拒绝会丢弃有效证据，盲目采纳则导致错误或不安全答案。因此需要模型具备选择性采纳相关信息、拒绝欺骗性内容的能力。

Method: 构建SelectBench基准与训练集，使用DAPO算法直接对Qwen3.5-4B进行后训练，采用两种奖励机制：确定性规则奖励（DAPO-Rule）和冻结的语义评判器（DAPO-DeepSeek）。

Result: SelectBench-v2测试集上严格成功率从基线22.46%提升至DAPO-Rule的25.54%和DAPO-DeepSeek的26.46%；减少了禁止内容的采纳并生成了更短、更聚焦的回答；但提示注入跟随方面未见改善，统计提升未通过Holm校正。

Conclusion: 选择性证据使用能力有方向性改善，但提示注入抵抗和统计稳健性仍是重要挑战，未来需要更强的奖励塑造或更多训练迭代。

Abstract: Retrieval-augmented large language models frequently face contexts that interleave useful evidence with misleading statements or instruction-like content. Blanket refusal discards valid evidence, whereas uncritical adoption yields incorrect or unsafe answers. The ability to selectively adopt relevant information while rejecting deceptive or harmful content is therefore critical for reliable deployment in real-world retrieval settings. We introduce SelectBench, a controlled benchmark and training set for selective evidence adoption, and post-train Qwen3.5-4B directly with DAPO using either deterministic rule rewards or a frozen semantic judge. On the corrected 325-example SelectBench-v2 test set, strict success rises from 22.46% for the original checkpoint to 25.54% with DAPO-Rule and 26.46% with DAPO-DeepSeek. Both trained policies reduce forbidden-content adoption and produce shorter, more focused responses, yet prompt-injection following does not improve. The paired gains are modest and fail to survive Holm correction, suggesting that stronger reward shaping or additional training iterations may be needed for more robust gains. DAPO-DeepSeek exhibits no material degradation on MMLU or clean HotpotQA, indicating that the post-training procedure preserves general capabilities. These results demonstrate a directional improvement in selective evidence use, while identifying injection resistance and statistical robustness as important remaining challenges for future work.

### [102] [Understanding the Impact of Linguistic Realization Choices on LLM Stance with Causal Tracing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20115)
*Langchen Huang,Sebastian Padó,Franziska Weeber*

TL;DR: 本文研究了语言构式（linguistic construction）能否系统性地改变大语言模型的决策，以及这种改变在模型内部的可定位因果关系。以政治立场判断为例，通过六种受控改写类型（保持或反转语义），发现模型对构式变化敏感，并通过激活修补（activation patching）定位到中后层解码器层的特定位置。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究关注词汇层面的提示敏感性，忽略了构式（construction）选择对LLM决策的系统性影响。作者希望探究语言构式是否以及如何导致模型输出偏移，并定位这种偏移在模型内部的因果来源。

Method: 扩展英文政治立场数据集，设计六种受控语言改写类型（意义保持与意义反转）。在四个开源模型上实验，测量立场不稳定程度。进一步使用激活修补（activation patching）技术，将原始语句的激活值替换到改写语句的前向传播中，检测哪些组件能恢复原始立场分布。

Result: 立场不稳定同时出现在意义保持和意义反转的改写中。激活修补结果表明，中后层解码器层（尤其是最终提示位置的块输出）提供了最强的恢复信号。

Conclusion: 语言构式能够系统性地影响LLM的政治立场判断，且这种影响主要源于模型的中后层解码器层，表明构式选择是一个被现有研究忽视但重要的鲁棒性因素。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are known to be sensitive to prompt and input formulations. However, existing studies have focused on lexical realization and largely ignored constructional choice. This paper studies whether linguistic construction can systematically shift LLM decisions and where these shifts can be causally localized inside the model. We use political stance judgment as a meaning-sensitive case study and extend an English political statements dataset, resulting in six controlled linguistic rewrite types that preserve or invert the meaning of a statement. Experiments on four open-weight models show that stance instability affect both meaning-preserving and meaning-inversing rewrites. Because output shifts reveal that rewrites affect stance, but not where in the model, we apply activation patching, where activations from the original statement are substituted into the forward pass for the rewritten statement and measure which components recover the original stance distribution. The results show that mid-to-late decoder layers, especially block outputs at the final prompt position, provide the strongest restoration signal.

### [103] [OpenSkillRisk: Benchmarking Agent Safety When Using Real-World Risky Third-Party Skills](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20121)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 从公开技能市场收集263个风险技能，分类为7种威胁类型，构建OpenSkillRisk基准。为每个技能配备标准化用户任务和沙箱环境，对三个主流CLI智能体框架和13个先进LLM进行综合实验。

Result: 即使最安全的配置仍有约17%的情况执行不安全操作；上下文相关和系统级风险最难规避；发现三种失败模式：风险识别失败、识别但未干预、超出用户意图执行指令。

Conclusion: 当前LLM智能体系统无法可靠处理风险技能，需要在LLM的风险推理能力和智能体框架的执行控制两方面进行改进。

Abstract: LLM-based agents leverage third-party skills to extend their capabilities in open-world scenarios. However, third-party skills can introduce extra security vulnerabilities, as seemingly harmless skills can contain latent safety risks that only emerge during actual execution. In this work, we conduct a systematic investigation into how well current agent systems recognize and avoid such risks. To support quantitative and qualitative evaluation, we construct OpenSkillRisk, a dedicated safety benchmark containing 263 risky skills collected from public skill marketplaces. We classify these skills into seven categories based on their threat types and pair each skill with a standardized user task and a corresponding sandbox for controlled evaluation. Distinct from prior benchmarks, OpenSkillRisk not only covers more realistic and diverse unsafe scenarios, but also provides a fine-grained analysis to diagnose the behavioral patterns of agents in such scenarios. We conduct comprehensive experiments covering three mainstream CLI agent frameworks and thirteen state-of-the-art LLMs. Experimental results show that no tested system handles risky skills reliably: even the safest configurations still execute unsafe actions in about 17% of cases. Context-dependent and system-level risks are especially difficult for current agent systems to avoid. Our behavioral analysis reveals three recurring failure patterns: agents may fail to recognize the risk, recognize it but fail to intervene before acting, or follow skill instructions beyond the user's intended scope. These findings highlight the need to improve both risk reasoning in LLMs and execution control in agent frameworks.

Abstract: The aim of this paper is twofold. First, it investigates whether newer generative models are getting better at pastiching contemporary artworks. We used five complementary computer vision models to capture texture, color, semantics, composition, and perceptual features through cosine distance in high-dimensional embedding spaces. The distances obtained show that the newer image generation model that we used has produced pastiches with improved semantic alignment and greater diversity than the model used in previous work. However, it was slightly less performant on shallow features such as color, texture, and perceptual adherence. Our findings confirm that artistic style is inherently multidimensional, and measuring it does not depend on any spatial architecture. Abstract: Full-parameter post-training of trillion-parameter-scale MoE models introduces substantial system-level challenges for large-scale distributed training, including severe memory pressure, non-overlapped communication overhead, and inefficient kernel execution. The resulting dataset contains 10K high-quality SFT samples spanning four task categories and three problem representations. The specialized model achieves the highest average zero-shot Pass@1 score among the evaluated models, reaching 71.81% and outperforming GPT-5.4-Mini and the base DeepSeek-V4-Flash model by 3.98 and 11.27 percentage points, respectively. ### [106] [Gotta Catch them all: the modes of Sycophancy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20146)
*Shreyans Jain,Alexandra Yost,Amirali Abdullah*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文通过分析948个社交压力情境下的三种奉承模式，发现奉承行为并非单一维度的倾向，而是具有表征和计算上不同模式的家族。从第14层开始，各模式在内部表征上完全线性可分，且依赖不同的注意力回路，对不同的输入反应最强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前对奉承行为的机械论研究多将其视为单一维度，可被统一增强或抑制。作者质疑这一假设，认为奉承行为可能存在多种机制模式，需要更细致的分析。

Method: 分析了三种假设的奉承模式在948个社交压力情境下的表现。使用文本分类器（准确率仅57.8%）测试输出相似性，并进一步分析内部表征的线性可分性、处理阶段、注意力回路及输入敏感性。

Result: 三种模式的输出极为相似（文本分类器准确率仅57.8%），但从第14层开始，其内部表征完全线性可分。各模式出现在不同的处理阶段，依赖不同的注意力回路，且对不同输入的反应强度不同。

Conclusion: 奉承行为不是单一的、整体的倾向，而是由表征和计算上不同的模式组成的结构化家族，这需要更精确的测量和干预方法。

Abstract: Large language models often align with users' beliefs at the expense of factual accuracy, a behavior known as sycophancy. Prior mechanistic studies largely treat sycophancy as a single behavioral dimension that can be uniformly amplified or suppressed. We challenge this assumption by analyzing three hypothesized modes of sycophancy across 948 social pressure situations. Although the modes produce highly similar outputs, with a text-only classifier achieving just 57.8 percent accuracy, their internal representations are perfectly linearly separable from layer 14 onward. We further find the modes emerge at different processing stages, rely on distinct attention circuitry, and fire strongest on different inputs. These results show that sycophancy is not a monolithic tendency, but a structured family of representationally and computationally distinct modes, motivating more precise measurement and intervention.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者通过三项分析实验，系统比较了不同算法与模型架构对语言模型概率计算的影响，揭示了LLM惊奇度并非中性可互换的指标。

Conclusion: 研究者应重新审视将不同LLM概率视为可互换的做法，在检验惊奇理论时需谨慎对待模型选择带来的表征与算法层面的承诺。

Abstract: Surprisal Theory is often characterized as a computational-level explanation per (Marr, 1982). We argue in this work that, even though a computational level narrative has been used to support "representation-agnostic research" within computational psycholinguistics, the movement toward black box systems embodied by large language models (LLMs) does not exempt modelers using the surprisal metric from the representational decisions required by computational-level characterizations. In fact, we argue that the uncritical use of LLM-surprisal obfuscates the representational and algorithmic-level commitments of different models. In three analyses, we show that the choice of algorithm and model architecture play significant roles in the computation of language model probabilities. We advise that researchers who wish to test Surprisal Theory re-evaluate the practice of treating large language model probabilities as interchangeable

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) can generate fluent Arabic answers, yet factual errors remain difficult to detect, localize, explain, and verify. The benchmark contains 2,400 expert-curated examples across four knowledge-intensive domains: Islamic knowledge, history, science, and geography. Each example pairs an Arabic question and a model-generated answer with a verified reference answer, a binary hallucination label, six candidate answers for factual verification, and, for hallucinated answers, character-level erroneous spans, human-written explanations, and macro and micro hallucination types.

Abstract: Culturally loaded translation poses unique challenges for machine translation (MT), as meanings are deeply embedded in socio-cultural contexts beyond surface linguistic forms. In this study, we systematically investigate the challenges posed by culturally loaded translation in LLM-based MT systems. ### [110] [Exposure is Optional: Learning Unlike Coordination in Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20251)
*Jiamu Luo,Shane Steinert-Threlkeld*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文通过滤除语料中所有"异类并列"实例来训练GPT-2，发现语言模型无需直接暴露即可泛化处理该结构，其机制类似于将并列元素视为同类范畴或通过删除操作实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究"异类并列"（unlike coordination）这一语言结构是否需要训练数据中的直接暴露才能被习得，还是可以从一般的组合能力中自然涌现。这既关乎语言学中关于并列结构的理论辩论，也有助于理解语言模型如何表示和习得语言结构。

Method: 采用Filtered-Corpus Training (FiCT)方法，从训练语料中移除所有异类并列实例，然后训练GPT-2模型。通过与在未过滤语料上训练的模型进行比较，评估模型在困惑度、语法判断以及内部表示上的表现。

Result: 直接暴露并非必要：过滤训练后的模型在异类并列上的困惑度和语法判断表现与未过滤模型相当。内部表示分析表明，模型处理异类并列时采用两种机制：将并列元素视为相似结构类别，或通过类似删除（deletion）的操作，这些机制仅从同类并列中即可习得。

Conclusion: 语言模型能够在不直接接触异类并列的情况下习得并泛化该结构，这为语言学中关于并列结构的理论争论提供了计算层面的新证据，同时增进了对语言模型内部语言表示机制的理解。

Abstract: Coordination, a fundamental linguistic structure, remains a subject of intense debate, and its exact nature continues to elude theoretical linguistics. A common view holds that only same-category constituents can be conjoined, which has been challenged by the many grammatical unlike coordinations found in natural language. Treating language models as a computational testbed, we investigate whether the acquisition of unlike coordination requires direct exposure in the training data, or whether it can emerge organically from general compositional abilities. Using Filtered-Corpus Training (FiCT), we train GPT-2 models on corpora from which all instances of unlike coordination have been removed. We find that direct exposure is not necessary: models trained on filtered data successfully generalize to unlike coordination, achieving perplexity and grammaticality judgments comparable to models trained on unfiltered text. Furthermore, our analyses of internal representations indicate that language models process unlike coordination by treating the conjoined elements as belonging to similar structural categories or through a mechanism akin to deletion, both of which appear learnable from exposure to alike coordination alone. This work contributes to the growing understanding of how language models internally represent linguistic structures, while also adding to the broader debate on coordination by showing how models generalize and process unlike coordination without direct exposure.

### [111] [The Maskability Index: Predicting Task-Objective Alignment in Pretrained Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20265)
*Ahmad Pouramini,Mahsa Afsharzadeh*

However, their performance depends on how closely the prompting strategy matches the objectives used during pretraining. We introduce the Maskability Index (MI), a quantitative metric that estimates whether a knowledge relation is better suited to masked-style prompting or prefix-style prompting in few-shot generation. MI is computed from differences in DepthRank scores between masked and unmasked templates, providing a principled measure of objective-template alignment. We evaluate MI on a diverse set of relations from the ATOMIC2020 knowledge base completion benchmark and show that it is positively correlated with downstream generation performance. ### [112] [Which Values Do LLMs Confuse? A Schwartz-Based Recognition Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20270)

TL;DR: 本文研究了LLM在具体情境中识别人类价值观的能力。基于Schwartz十种基本价值观，构建了1000条俄语情境文本，评估了21个指令微调LLM。结果显示：Top-1准确率0.683，Top-3准确率0.892；邻近价值观构成了50.9%的语义错误；发现了八种系统性的方向性混淆（如普遍主义→仁爱、传统→遵从等），且严重程度因模型而异。

Conclusion: LLM价值观识别评估应综合使用精确准确率、排序恢复和方向性错误分析三种指标，以全面刻画模型能力与系统性偏差。

Abstract: Large language models are increasingly evaluated through the values they endorse, but such evaluations presuppose that models can identify the value expressed in a concrete situation. We study this prerequisite as controlled top-1 recognition over Schwartz's ten basic values. Our evaluation set contains 1,000 Russian situational texts, balanced across the ten values and independently labeled by two human annotators per item. We evaluate 21 instruction-tuned LLM runs under a fixed ranked-response protocol; 20 runs with reliable outputs form the semantic panel. Pooled Acc@1 is 0.683 and Acc@3 is 0.892, showing that models often locate the correct motivational region while ranking close alternatives unstably. Adjacent values account for 50.9% of semantic errors, compared with 24.4% under a checkpoint-specific null. Eight directed confusions recur across checkpoints and human-confirmed subsets. Several are strongly asymmetric, including Universalism to Benevolence, Tradition to Conformity, and Security to Power, whereas Stimulation-Hedonism forms a bidirectional boundary. Their severity is checkpoint-specific and can bias higher-order value profiles. The results motivate value-recognition evaluation that combines exact accuracy, ranked recovery, and directed error analysis.

### [113] [Sound Probabilistic Safety Bounds for Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20286)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法难以在大语言模型（LLM）中有效评估生成有害输出的极低概率，缺乏严格且可计算的统计下界，亟需一种能提供形式化保证的评估方法。

Result: 实验证明，该方法能在实际中计算非平凡的下界，即使真实有害概率极低时也有效，且下界是可靠的（即严格小于实际有害概率），在先进LLM上验证了有效性。

Abstract: We propose a novel framework for computing rigorous bounds on the probability that a large language model (LLM) generates harmful output to a given prompt. We study a new application of the Clopper-Pearson confidence intervals to obtain probably approximately correct (PAC) bounds for this problem. As our main technical contribution, we propose an algorithm that leverages features in the latent space to prioritize exploring branches in the auto-regressive generation tree that are more likely to produce harmful outputs. Our approach in particular enables the efficient computation of useful lower bounds, even in scenarios where the true harm probability is extremely small, and crucially, the obtained lower bounds are sound, i.e., formally proven to be less than the actual harmfulness probability: our experimental results demonstrate the effectiveness of our method by computing non-trivial lower bounds on state-of-the-art LLMs. This study newly enables the evaluation and statistical certification of LLMs.

### [114] [PyroDash: Cost-Efficient Token-Level Small-Large Language Model Collaborative Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20327)
*Niqi Lyu,Pengtao Shi,Wei Qiu,Jianlin Zhong,Sicong Xia,Jianyao Ma,Yicheng Ding*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: PyroDash提出了一种令牌级的小模型-大模型协同推理框架，通过让小模型（SLM）在生成过程中自主发射控制令牌决定是否向大模型（LLM）求助，在保持推理性能的同时显著降低推理成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型（LLM）推理能力强但服务成本高，小语言模型（SLM）成本低但处理复杂问题时可靠性不足。如何在两者间实现成本感知的协同推理是一个关键问题。

Method: 提出三阶段训练流程：1）控制令牌嵌入学习；2）面向卸载的监督微调；3）基于GRPO的成本感知对齐。SLM在生成时自主决定是否发射控制令牌触发LLM辅助，通过单次交接完成协作。

Result: 在5个数学推理基准上，λ=0.05时准确率64.04%（超LLM基线6.36个百分点），成本降低20.4%；λ=0.6时准确率54.55%，LLM令牌占比仅1.90%，每次示例仅调用0.012次LLM，总成本从49.36美元降至1.78美元。

Conclusion: 学习得到的令牌级交接机制能有效减少LLM使用量，同时保持甚至提升强推理性能，为SLM-LLM协同推理提供了一个灵活的成本-精度权衡方案。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) provide strong reasoning capabilities but are expensive to serve at scale, whereas small language models (SLMs) are cheaper but less reliable on difficult problems. We introduce PyroDash, a cost-aware framework for token-level SLM-LLM collaborative inference. During generation, the SLM decides whether to request assistance by emitting a control token. A Collaborate Engine then sends the query and partial reasoning trace to a frozen LLM for completion through a single handoff. The policy is internalized in the SLM, requiring neither a separate router, LLM retraining, nor access to LLM logits. PyroDash trains the SLM in three stages: control-token embedding learning, offloading-oriented supervised fine-tuning, and cost-aware alignment with Group Relative Policy Optimization. Its reward balances answer accuracy against inference cost normalized by LLM-only inference. Across five mathematical reasoning benchmarks, PyroDash supports different accuracy-cost operating points. With $λ=0.05$, it achieves 64.04 percent average accuracy, 6.36 percentage points above the LLM-only baseline, while reducing cost by 20.4 percent. With $λ=0.6$, it achieves 54.55 percent accuracy with a 1.90 percent LLM token ratio and 0.012 LLM calls per example, reducing total cost from USD 49.36 to USD 1.78. These results show that learned token-level handoffs can reduce LLM use while preserving strong reasoning performance.

</details>


### [115] [Generative AI floods and dilutes the market for books](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20349)
*Tuhin Chakrabarty,Xinyue Liu,Jane C. Ginsburg,Paramveer Dhillon*

TL;DR: 生成式AI可以以近乎零成本创作长篇小说。通过对2023-2026年Amazon平台上14,419本自出版类型小说的AI文本检测与日销售数据匹配分析，发现含大量AI文本（>25%）的书籍在目录中占比大但销售额占比小，却正占据原本由非AI书籍把持的头部位置。AI书籍数量呈19.2倍增长，而季度收入仅增长8.9倍，每本书收入下降。这类书籍通过规模而非质量重塑创意市场。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 挑战"AI生成书籍是低质量垃圾、买家会忽视"的普遍假设，实证检验AI生成作品在商业市场上的实际影响力。

Method: 对2023-2026年间Amazon上14,419本自出版类型小说进行全文本AI检测，并与截至2026年6月的日销售数据匹配分析。

Result: 含大量AI文本的书籍目录占比大但销售额占比小，却正在增长销售份额并占据原本由非AI书籍把持的头部排名位置。AI书籍数量增长（19.2倍）远超收入增长（8.9倍），每本书收入下降。非AI书籍在AI渗透率高的类型中损失最大。头部AI书籍的语言更独特，收入越高重叠度越大。

Conclusion: 生成式AI可以通过规模而非质量重塑创意市场，这对版权侵权抗辩中的合理使用市场影响评估具有直接意义。

Abstract: Generative AI can produce book-length works of fiction at near-zero cost. These books are often dismissed as low-quality ``slop'' that buyers will ignore, and are assumed to carry little commercial weight. We test that assumption with full-text AI detection across 14,419 self-published genre-fiction books sold on Amazon from 2023 to 2026, matched to daily sales records through June 2026. None of these books disclose whether or not they contain AI-produced content. We find that books for which we detected substantial AI text ($>$ 25\%) make up a large share of the catalog but a smaller share of sales. Even so, they reach commercial scale, winning a growing share of sales over time and taking more of the scarce top-rank positions once held by books with no detected AI text. Over this period, the number of books with observed sales in a quarter grew 19.2-fold, while quarterly revenue grew only 8.9-fold. The market therefore added selling books faster than it added revenue, and revenue per selling book fell across most genres. Books with no AI text lose the most ground in genres with high AI diffusion, and most of all where Kindle Unlimited availability is high. Among top-selling books, those with substantial AI text draw on more distinctive language from existing books than do books with no AI text; for these books overlap rises with revenue, a gradient we do not detect for books with no AI text. Generative AI can thus reshape a creative market through scale rather than quality. Our results bear directly on the market-effect question at the center of the fair use defense to copyright infringement.

</details>


### [116] [Notes to Self: Can LLMs Benefit from Experiential Abstractions?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20372)
*Chang Liu,Xinyu Li,Artur Dubrawski*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出让LLM从解题轨迹中提取自然语言抽象（如策略、提醒），构建可检索库，并通过推理时检索或强化学习增强训练提示，从而提升数学和逻辑推理性能。自我提取的抽象与教师提取的效果相当，且能跨数据集和模型迁移。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索大语言模型能否像人类一样从经验中提炼可复用的抽象（如策略、警示），并利用这些抽象逐步提升问题解决能力。

Method: 从MATH训练集的解题轨迹中，由强教师或LLM自身提取自然语言抽象，建立可检索库；采用两种使用方式：(1)推理时检索相关抽象作为辅助；(2)将抽象增强到训练提示中进行强化学习。

Result: 经验性抽象显著提升了LLM在数学和逻辑推理基准上的性能；自我提取的抽象与教师提取的效果相当；该框架可迁移到其他数据集和模型。

Conclusion: LLM能够像人类利用蒸馏经验一样提取和应用经验性抽象，从而提升推理能力。

Abstract: Humans distill experience into reusable abstractions, e.g., strategies and cautionary reminders, and apply them to gradually solve problems more effectively. We study whether Large Language Models (LLMs) can similarly benefit from such experiential abstractions. From LLMs' solution traces on the MATH training set, a stronger teacher or the LLMs themselves extract natural-language abstractions into a retrievable library. We explore two usage modes: (1) inference-time retrieval and (2) reinforcement learning (RL) with abstraction-augmented training prompts. Experiential abstractions improve LLM performance on mathematical and logical reasoning benchmarks. Self-extracted abstractions match teacher-extracted ones, and our abstraction usage framework can transfer to other datasets and models. These findings suggest LLMs can extract and apply experiential abstractions much as humans leverage distilled experience.

### [117] [LKValues: Aligning Large Language Models with Sri Lankan Societal Values](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20410)
*Nethmi Muthugala,Supryadi,Surangika Ranathunga,Nisansa de Silva,Ruijie Tao,Ovindu Gunatunga,Pengyun Zhu,Shaowei Zhang,Jingting Zheng,Deyi Xiong*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出LKValues，首个基于调查的斯里兰卡价值观对齐资源套件，包含150k条指令语料库和1k条评估基准，发现主流LLM在斯里兰卡文化价值观对齐上存在显著缺口，微调后可减少无效输出和跨语言差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM价值观对齐存在西方中心主义偏见，忽视斯里兰卡等多元语言社会独特的本土文化价值观，且缺乏针对僧伽罗语的评估基准。

Method: 通过三语（僧伽罗语、泰米尔语、英语）对205名受访者进行问卷调查，结合全球框架与LLM引导的本土构念，提炼出40项多数认可的社会价值观；据此构建僧伽罗-英语新闻衍生指令语料库LKvaluesIT（15万条情景实例）和评估基准LKvaluesBench（1000条实例）。

Result: 在专有和开源LLM上评估发现，更新更大的模型仍存在低资源语言和文化价值观对齐缺口；对Qwen3.5-4B-Base、Qwen3.5-9B-Base、Aya-Expanse-8B-Base微调后，Qwen系列在英语和僧伽罗语上表现提升，减少了无效输出和跨语言差异，但效果依赖模型家族。

Conclusion: LKValues在嵌入斯里兰卡价值观上有效，为低资源、国家特定多元价值观对齐提供了可复现的流水线。

Abstract: Value alignment of Large Language Models (LLMs) has been shown to be culturally biased toward Western norms. This results in the mishandling of local values in multilingual societies such as Sri Lanka that have their unique cultural dynamics. Existing benchmarks overlook Sri Lankan-contextualized values in its official language Sinhala, hindering culturally sensitive evaluation and fine-tuning. To bridge this gap, we propose LKValues, the first survey-grounded resource suite for Sri Lankan value alignment. From a trilingual survey of 205 respondents, blending adapted global frameworks and LLM-elicited local constructs, we derive 40 majority-endorsed societal values. Using these values, we construct LKvaluesIT, a Sinhala-English news-derived instruction corpus containing 150k scenario-based instances, and LKvaluesBench, a value-sensitive evaluation benchmark of 1,000 instances. We evaluate a set of proprietary and open-weight LLMs with LKvaluesBench. We fine-tune three open-weight base models (Qwen3.5-4B-Base, Qwen3.5-9B-Base, and Aya-Expanse-8B-Base). Our experiments show that newer and larger LLMs still exhibit low-resource and cultural value-alignment gaps. LKValues fine-tuning improves Qwen-family models in English and Sinhala, reducing invalid outputs and cross-lingual disparities, though gains remain model-family dependent. These highlight LKValues efficacy in embedding Sri Lankan values, offering a replicable pipeline for low-resource, country-specific pluralist value alignment. The dataset is publicly available at https://github.com/NextME14/LKValues.

Method: 提出PRTA框架，包含：1) LLM作为中央规划器，负责高层推理和个性化工具选择；2) 多个传统推荐模型作为工具，负责全排序评分；3) 反思机制，基于用户画像和候选排名列表评估和比较工具。

Abstract: Although large language models (LLMs) have recently gained traction in recommender systems due to their strong reasoning capabilities and extensive world knowledge, previous LLM-based agents suffer from hallucination and context-length limitations, and thus are not suitable for full-ranking recommendation tasks. To circumvent these limitations through architectural design rather than modifying the LLM itself, we propose an agent-based recommendation framework, memory-based $\textbf{P}$ersonalized $\textbf{R}$ecommendation $\textbf{T}$ool learning via autonomous language $\textbf{A}$gents (PRTA), in which an LLM acts as a central planner interacting with multiple recommendation models as tools. The LLM-based agent is responsible for high-level reasoning and personalized tool selection, while traditional recommendation models perform full-ranking scoring, leveraging their scalability in modeling behavioral patterns. To support personalized tool selection, we design reflection mechanisms that enable the agent to evaluate and compare tools for each user based on user profiles and candidate ranked lists. Extensive experiments across three public datasets demonstrate the superiority of \modelname over traditional recommendation and LLM-based baselines in improving full-ranking recommendation performance.

### [120] [Zero-Observation User Reactivation with Gap-Driven Dimensional Gating](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19802)
*Jiandong Ding,Tianying Liu,Fuyuan Liu,Huijie Qin,Tiandeng Wu*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文针对序列推荐中用户长时间无交互（零观察重新激活）问题，提出轻量级输出层插件DeltaGate，利用时间间隔和个性化表示动态路由特征，在冻结骨干网络下显著提升长间隔推荐性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有序列推荐模型依赖连续行为数据，但用户可能数月或数年无交互，导致推荐性能随间隔时间增长而显著下降。现有方法无法有效处理这种"零观察重新激活"场景。

Method: 提出DeltaGate，一个轻量级输出层插件，保持骨干网络冻结，通过门控机制将每个表示维度在个性化历史与学习到的零初始化全局先验之间进行路由，门控同时基于时间间隔Δt和个性化表示。

Result: 在>365天间隔下，DG-SASRec Hit@10达0.047（基线0.031），DG-BERT4Rec达0.046（基线0.025），仅66K可训练参数（2-4%开销），端到端重训练虽精度更高但改变骨干嵌入，而冻结插件几乎无骨干漂移。

Conclusion: DeltaGate能有效应对长时间间隔的零观察重新激活问题，在保持骨干网络不变的同时显著提升性能，且参数效率极高。

Abstract: Sequential recommendation (SR) models capture continuously observed behavior, but a returning user may have no interactions for months or years. We define this setting as Zero-Observation Reactivation: the user has a pre-gap history, while the platform observes no behavioral signals during a macro-gap Delta t. Under a chronologically aligned Gap-Synthesize Protocol on three Amazon datasets (Video Games, CDs & Vinyl, and Movies & TV), Hit@10 decreases monotonically across the evaluated gap buckets and reaches its lowest level beyond one year. The pattern appears across recurrent, unidirectional, and bidirectional SR backbones.
  We propose DeltaGate, a lightweight output-layer plugin that keeps the backbone frozen and routes each representation dimension between the personalized history and a learned, zero-initialized global prior. The gate is conditioned jointly on Delta t and the personalized representation. In a controlled diagnostic, we hold the personalized representation fixed and vary Delta t to isolate the trained gate's response to the gap input. In the >365d Video Games bucket, DG-SASRec reaches 0.047 Hit@10 versus 0.031 for SASRec, while DG-BERT4Rec reaches 0.046 versus 0.025 for BERT4Rec, with 66K trainable parameters (2--4% overhead). End-to-end retraining attains higher absolute accuracy but changes the backbone embeddings; the frozen plugin preserves zero backbone drift, uses about 40x fewer trainable parameters, and retains observable dimension-wise routing. The source code is available at https://github.com/jdding/DeltaGate.

</details>


### [121] [Using Hierarchical Controlled Vocabularies to Understand CLIP Retrieval Failures in Historical Photo Collections](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19836)
*Ratan Sebastian,Anett Hoppe,Christoph Rippe,Ralph Ewerth*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文研究CLIP在GLAM机构图像检索中的表现差异，发现视觉一致性与文本-图像对齐几乎不相关，且可分离不同失败模式；层级深度影响微调效果，浅层术语获益更多。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: GLAM机构使用AAT等受控词表组织图像，但CLIP等视觉-语言模型在内容检索中的表现存在差异。现有研究仅从概念抽象度、频率等角度解释，未从AAT的结构属性（如根面类型、层级深度）分析差异成因。

Method: 在三组历史摄影数据集中，以AAT术语标注，提取CLIP嵌入空间中的视觉一致性（术语图像聚类程度）和文本-图像对齐（标签与聚类中心距离），并分析其与根面类型、层级深度等结构属性的关系，同时对比微调前后的检索性能变化。

Result: 1) 视觉一致性与文本-图像对齐几乎不相关，且能分离不同失败模式；2) 图像聚类紧密但标签远离的术语检索效果最差；3) 根面类型显著区分视觉一致性，但检索指标与结构属性无显著相关；4) 微调提升检索性能，但对浅层术语的文本-图像对齐提升更大，超越词频解释力。

Conclusion: AAT的结构属性（根面类型、层级深度）能部分解释CLIP在GLAM图像检索中的表现差异，微调可改善但受益不均；未来应结合受控词表结构设计更适配的视觉-语言模型检索策略。

Abstract: GLAM institutions (Galleries, Libraries, Archives, and Museums) organise image access using controlled vocabularies such as the Art and Architecture Thesaurus (AAT). For content-based image retrieval in these settings, vision-language models like CLIP are increasingly used, but their performance varies. This variation is known to relate to measures like concept abstraction and concept frequency. However, no prior work explains this variation in terms of the structural properties of vocabularies like the AAT that GLAM professionals already use. The AAT groups concepts into broad facets (Objects, Activities, Agents, etc.) and arranges terms hierarchically within them. In this paper, we ask whether two structural properties (root facet type and hierarchy depth) explain where CLIP retrieval succeeds and fails, and where fine-tuning helps. Across three historical photographic collections annotated with AAT terms, we examine visual coherence (whether a term's photographs cluster in CLIP's embedding space), text-image alignment (whether its label is near that cluster), and standard retrieval measures, which conflate the two. We find that visual coherence and text-image alignment are nearly uncorrelated across terms and jointly separate distinct failure modes. Terms whose photographs cluster tightly but whose label is distant from the cluster retrieve poorly in every collection, in two of three collections even worse than terms that fail on both metrics. We also show that while retrieval metrics do not correlate significantly with either structural property, root facet type does significantly separate categories with varying visual coherence. Finally, we find that fine-tuning improves retrieval overall, but its gains favour shallower terms in the hierarchy, where text-image alignment improves most, beyond what concept frequency explains.

</details>


### [122] [UniRank: Benchmarking Ranking Models for Unified Sequential Modeling and Feature Interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19987)
*Honghao Li,Xianquan Wang,Zibin Zhang,Yi Zhang,Kangyi Lin,Yiwen Zhang*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文提出UniRank，一个面向统一序列建模与特征交互的排序模型开源基准平台，提供标准化评估、高效训练工具和15个模型在5个大规模公开数据集上的可复现基准结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有统一序列建模与特征交互的排序模型多依赖闭源数据和工业基础设施，导致可复现性差、阻碍学术研究（如规模化法则、长序列建模、多任务排序）的进展。

Method: 构建UniRank基准，采用时序逐点自回归监督、标准化多任务评估；提供PyTorch工具包（含分布式数据并行训练、算子优化、混合精度训练、注意力优化等）；在5个大规模公开数据集上基准测试15个代表性模型。

Result: 最大数据集超7亿实例、最长行为序列超10^5交互；成功复现并对比15个模型，降低硬件需求，缩小学术与工业排序研究的差距。

Conclusion: UniRank为排序模型研究提供了可复现、生产导向且易用的基准平台，有助于研究人员、从业者和初学者在有限算力下研究规模化法则，推动学术与工业的融合。

Abstract: Ranking is a core stage in online advertising and recommender systems. Modern ranking models increasingly unify sequential modeling and feature interaction, yet many advances rely on proprietary data, closed implementations, and large-scale industrial infrastructure. This setting limits reproducible comparison and hinders academic study of scaling laws, long-sequence modeling, and multi-task ranking. To address these limitations, this paper proposes UniRank, an open benchmark for ranking models that unify sequential modeling and feature interaction. UniRank uses chronological pointwise autoregressive supervision, standardizes evaluation across feedback tasks, and provides a PyTorch toolkit with Distributed Data Parallel training, operator optimization, mixed-precision training, attention optimization, and other efficiency techniques that reduce hardware requirements. We benchmark 15 representative unified ranking models on five large-scale public datasets from short-video, advertising, and e-commerce platforms, with the largest dataset containing over 700 million instances and the longest behavior sequence exceeding 10^5 interactions. UniRank provides a reproducible basis for comparing unified ranking models, studying scaling laws under limited compute, and narrowing the gap between academic and industrial ranking research. We believe UniRank benefits researchers, practitioners, and beginners through reproducible experiments, production-oriented evaluation, and accessible implementations. Code and data are available at https://github.com/salmon1802/UniRank.

</details>

### [123] [Understanding Developer Pain Points in Federated Learning: Insights from Stack Overflow and GitHub](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19621)
*Sahand Saed,Khairul Alam,Banani Roy*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文通过分析495个Stack Overflow帖子和9,116个GitHub问题/PR，系统研究了联邦学习开发者面临的九大Stack Overflow主题和十三大GitHub主题挑战，发现环境配置、API兼容性、训练不稳定性、评估正确性和隐私保护集成是主要痛点，其中"如何"类问题占主导，反映了对程序性指导的强烈需求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 联邦学习系统在构建和运维中面临分布式执行、框架快速演进及隐私合规等困难，但目前缺乏对开发者实际挑战的系统性实证研究。作者旨在通过大规模公开数据挖掘，识别开发者痛点并推动FL系统可用性的改进。

Method: 采用混合方法：1) 从Stack Overflow（495条）和GitHub（9,116个issues/PR）收集数据；2) 使用BERTopic进行主题建模；3) 采用未解决率和中位解决时间作为难度指标；4) 对问题意图进行分类（"如何"、"为什么"等）。

Result: 识别出9个Stack Overflow主题和13个GitHub主题；主要困难集中在环境配置与依赖兼容性、API变更与迁移、非IID数据下的训练不稳定、评估与指标正确性、隐私保护机制集成；"如何"类问题占比最高；部分主题（如TFF安装、联邦特征工程）具有高未解决率和长解决时间。

Conclusion: 研究为FL框架设计者、文档作者和教育者提供了可操作的建议，并展示了一种可扩展的持续监控开发者痛点的研究方法。虽然受限于公开讨论和部分框架，但该方法可用于持续改善FL系统的可用性、可靠性和可部署性。

Abstract: Federated Learning (FL) enables collaborative model training without centralizing raw data, but building and operating FL systems remains difficult due to distributed execution, rapidly evolving frameworks, and privacy and governance requirements. In this paper, we present an empirical study of FL developer challenges by independently analyzing 495 Stack Overflow posts and 9,116 GitHub issues and pull requests from 92 FL-related projects. Using BERTopic-based topic modeling and difficulty indicators such as unresolved rates and median resolution time, we characterize recurring problem areas and compare how they manifest across the two support platforms, Stack Overflow and GitHub. Our analysis surfaces nine dominant Stack Overflow topics and thirteen GitHub topics, with persistent difficulties concentrated in environment setup and dependency compatibility, API breakages and migration, training instability under non-IID data, evaluation and metric correctness, and the integration of privacy-preserving mechanisms. We also categorize posts by question intent to understand the kinds of help developers seek; this intent analysis shows that "How"-type questions dominate, reflecting strong demand for procedural guidance. Several topics, such as "TFF Installation and Environment Compatibility" and "Federated Feature Engineering and SecureBoost Issues," exhibit high unresolved rates and long resolution times, suggesting shortcomings in tooling, documentation, and debugging support. Based on these findings, we provide actionable implications for FL framework designers, documentation authors, and educators. Although our results are constrained to public discussions and a subset of widely discussed frameworks, the study offers a scalable method for continuously monitoring developer pain points and improving the usability, reliability, and deployability of FL systems.

</details>


### [124] [PerfAgent: Profiler-Guided Iterative Refinement for Repository-Level Code Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19653)
*Ryan Deng,Yuanzhe Liu,Bastian Lipka,Yao Ma,Xuhao Chen,Tim Kaler,Jatin Ganhotra*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: PerfAgent是一个性能优化智能体，它利用分析器指导和验证器循环，帮助大语言模型智能体在仓库级代码优化任务中超越简单加速，实现专家级别的优化效果。在GSO和SWE-fficiency-Lite两个基准上，PerfAgent将匹配专家优化的补丁率分别从19.6%提升至39.2%，从26%提升至74%。

Method: PerfAgent采用分析器指导（profiler-guided）与验证器循环（verifier-in-the-loop）的工作流程：通过性能分析器定位真正的热点瓶颈，利用验证器持续反馈，让智能体不满足于第一个通过的补丁，而是基于分析器证据而非单纯计时来决定下一步优化方向。

Conclusion: PerfAgent通过引入分析器指导和验证器循环的反馈机制，显著提升了LLM智能体在仓库级代码优化任务中的表现，证明了更好的反馈比简单增加采样次数更有效。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM) agents now perform well on correctness-oriented repository-level tasks, including SWE-Bench issue resolution and feature implementation in real codebases. However, they still struggle with repository-level code optimization, which requires preserving behavior while improving runtime performance. Passing tests is not enough in this setting; a patch must preserve behavior, implement code optimization, and approach expert speedups. Current agents often miss bottlenecks hidden behind abstraction layers and native extensions, stop after shallow speedups, or insufficiently test the code patches that thus may silently break edge cases. We present PerfAgent, a profiler-guided, verifier-in-the-loop workflow that gives an off-the-shelf coding agent the feedback needed to find real hotspots, improve beyond the first passing patch, and use profiler evidence rather than timing alone to decide what to optimize next. On two challenging optimization benchmarks, GSO and SWE-fficiency-Lite, PerfAgent more than doubles the rate of expert-matching patches over OpenHands with GPT-5.1, improving from 19.6% to 39.2% on GSO and from 26% to 74% on SWE-fficiency-Lite. It also surpasses an oracle best-of-five baseline at substantially lower cost, showing that the gains come from better feedback rather than additional test-time sampling.

Although large language models (LLMs) have shown strong code generation capabilities, their use for automated glue code generation remains unexplored. This task requires reasoning over underspecified behavior, related BDD artifacts, and large project codebases. AutoGlue follows a behavior-first workflow that separates behavior interpretation, context retrieval, and code generation. Ablation results show that behavior interpretation and project-aware context retrieval both contribute substantially to generation quality. These findings demonstrate that LLMs can effectively connect natural-language behavior specifications with project code and support specification-driven software development.

Abstract: Zero-Knowledge Ethereum Virtual Machines (zkEVMs) secure Ethereum rollups by generating zero-knowledge proofs that guarantee off-chain execution correctness. However, subtle implementation bugs (e.g., incorrect gas accounting) can lead to valid proofs certifying semantically faulty states, thereby silently defeating cryptographic guarantees. Formal verification via SMT solvers can prevent this, but is bottlenecked by specification: current zkEVM development practice lacks automated methods to translate Rust opcode handlers into verification models. Current practices rely on unsustainable manual specifications, while LLM-based approaches suffer from hallucination and lack formal guarantees. To address this, we propose VeriSynth, a framework that synthesizes executable Python/Z3 verification models from Rust zkEVM code. VeriSynth enforces a hybrid paradigm: an LLM acts strictly as a formalization frontend to translate code into symbolic constraints, while an SMT solver serves as the correctness arbiter. To handle complex multi-component state transitions, VeriSynth integrates semantic decomposition, retrieval-grounded prompting, and verification-guided auto-repair into a closed-loop pipeline. We evaluate VeriSynth on the first source-level zkEVM verification benchmark, encompassing both correct and faulty opcode implementations. VeriSynth achieves a bug detection rate of over 90%, substantially outperforming direct and conversational LLM baselines, as well as a production-grade handwritten mutation-testing suite. ### [128] [Beyond Fail-to-Pass: Iterative Hardening of Co-Generated Bug Reproduction Tests and Fixes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19843)
*Yuhao Tan,Zhibang Yang,Fangkai Yang,Yuan Yao,Yu Kang,Lu Wang,Pu Zhao,Xin Zhang,Xiaoxing Ma,Qingwei Lin,Saravan Rajmohan,Dongmei Zhang*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 论文提出CoHarden框架，通过区分严格与宽松的错误重现测试(BRT)，采用共生成与迭代加固策略，在SWE-bench Verified上实现69.4%修复成功率，超越现有基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有BRT评估仅依赖F->P标准，但该标准无法区分"宽松"和"严格"的测试。宽松测试虽能捕获bug症状，却会允许错误补丁通过，导致下游修复效果不佳。此外，共生成过程中存在测试-修复错误耦合问题，即使两者都错，F->P检查仍可能通过。

Method: 提出CoHarden框架：(1)先基于bug报告生成测试，再生成修复补丁；(2)定义Lax信号作为循环内收敛准则；(3)迭代加固测试和修复，对抗变异补丁，直到测试不再允许宽松回归。

Result: 在SWE-bench Verified上达到69.4% Resolved和78.9% F->P，相比最强的纯修复基线和共生成基线，Resolved分别提升+9.6和+7.9个百分点，且在不同LLM主干和基准上表现一致。

Conclusion: F->P标准本身不足以评估BRT质量，需区分严格与宽松测试。CoHaven通过迭代加固有效消除宽松测试，显著提升自动程序修复的成功率。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have made automated program repair (APR) increasingly practical for real-world bugs, but repairing directly from bug reports remains underconstrained. Bug reproduction tests (BRTs) help close this gap by turning a bug report into an executable, bug-specific signal that can guide repair and validate candidate patches. Existing work has therefore studied BRT generation as a core subproblem in APR and mainly evaluates a generated BRT using the fail-to-pass (F->P) criterion, which requires the test to fail on the buggy code but pass on the golden fix. We show that F->P alone is insufficient when the goal of a BRT is to improve downstream repair. In particular, some F->P BRTs are lax, reproducing the observed symptom yet still admitting plausible-but-incorrect patches. We formalize this missing quality dimension by separating F->P BRTs into rigorous and lax ones, and show empirically that only the former consistently improve repair success. We further find that co-generation introduces test--fix error coupling, where the in-trajectory fail-to-pass (F->P) check can pass even when both the generated patch and generated test are wrong. Based on these findings, we propose CoHarden, a co-generation framework that uses the Lax signal as an in-loop convergence criterion. CoHarden first generates a test before any fix, then iteratively hardens the test and fix against surviving mutation patches until the generated test no longer admits Lax regressions. Experiments show that CoHarden reaches 69.4% Resolved and 78.9% F->P on SWE-bench Verified, outperforming the strongest fix-only and cogeneration baselines by +9.6 and +7.9 percentage points in Resolved, respectively, with consistent gains across LLM backbones and benchmarks.

</details>

*Feng Luo,Jiachen Liu,Cuiyun Gao,Jia Feng,Kui Liu*

Abstract: The migration of legacy C programs to Rust has become an important direction for improving software memory safety while alleviating the high cost of manual rewriting. Leveraging large language models (LLMs) for automated C-to-Rust translation has emerged as a promising direction. However, existing LLM-based approaches remain limited. On the one hand, LLMs exhibit limited capability in identifying Rust-specific rules, and inadequate handling of Rust syntax often results in incorrect translations. On the other hand, existing LLMs often struggle to accurately capture the semantics of complex code, resulting in incorrect translations. To address these challenges, we propose a Translation fRAmework Via rule-guided reasoning and rEinforcement Learning, namely TRAVEL, consisting of two modules. The first module employs Monte Carlo Tree Search (MCTS)-based reasoning path construction guided by Rust-specific rules, steering the search toward translation steps that respect the syntactic rules that LLMs frequently violate. The second module introduces reinforcement learning that couples execution feedback with reasoning-quality signals, encouraging the model to construct reasoning paths that accurately capture program semantics, thereby ensuring that the generated Rust code preserves the intended behavior of the original C program. We evaluate TRAVEL on three datasets: xCodeEval (a public benchmark), OS-Bench (functions collected from the Linux kernel), and HW-Bench (an industrial dataset from Huawei). On xCodeEval, TRAVEL outperforms all baselines across three backbone LLMs. In particular, compared to the strongest prompting baseline IRENE, TRAVEL improves computational accuracy (CA) by 26.22% and compilation success rate (CSR) by 18.77%. On HW-Bench and OS-Bench, TRAVEL further improves CSR by 18.28% and 16.51%, respectively, while reducing unsafe rate (UR) by 13.06% and 13.08%, respectively.

### [130] [SequenceFI: Non-intrusive Temporal Fault Injection for Microservice Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20050)
*Yuzhen Tan,Jian Wang,Bing Li,Shaolin Tan*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出SequenceFI，一个非侵入式的时间敏感故障注入框架，通过监控消息事件、传播时间证据并仅在时间守卫满足时触发故障，解决了微服务系统中时序依赖故障难以复现的问题，在450次试验中实现了100%的时序成功率，并将搜索时间减少95.91%。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: SequenceFI框架通过三个关键设计实现时间故障注入：1）观察消息级别的发送和接收事件；2）沿请求执行传播紧凑的时间证据；3）仅在满足发生率敏感的时间守卫时触发故障。同时从追踪中自动合成时间守卫，减少穷举枚举配置的需求，无需修改应用代码或序列化库。

Conclusion: SequenceFI有效解决了微服务系统中时序依赖故障的复现问题，通过非侵入式的时间守卫机制实现了高精度的时间故障注入，大幅提升了配置搜索效率，验证了其在时序故障复现方面的有效性和实用性。

Abstract: Fault injection is widely used to evaluate the resilience of microservice systems, where client requests often span multiple services and execution stages. Existing request-level techniques usually control where and what faults are injected, but not when they are activated within a distributed execution. This limitation makes it difficult to reproduce timing-dependent failures, such as failures after state-changing side effects, order-sensitive concurrent responses, and partial failures among repeated downstream calls. This paper presents SequenceFI, a non-intrusive framework for temporal fault injection in microservice systems. SequenceFI observes message-level send and receive events, propagates compact temporal evidence along request executions, and triggers faults only when occurrence-sensitive temporal guards are satisfied. It further synthesizes temporal guards from traces, reducing the need for exhaustive enumeration of temporal fault-injection configurations, while requiring no modifications to application code or serialization libraries. We implement SequenceFI on Kubernetes and evaluate it on four widely used microservice benchmarks. Across nine temporal-fault scenarios and 450 valid trials, SequenceFI achieves 100.0\% temporal success without premature or multiple injections, finds effective configurations in one attempt on average, and reduces aggregate end-to-end search time by 95.91\% compared with H-Random.

### [131] [Multi-stage Dynamic Selection for Cross-Project Defect Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20151)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统跨项目缺陷预测方法因训练项目与目标项目之间存在分布偏移（distribution shift），导致模型性能严重下降。现有方法通常对整个目标项目使用同一组分类器，缺乏对模块级差异的适应性。

Method: 提出两阶段多分类器系统（MCS）选择框架：第一阶段（项目级选择）评估多个候选MCS配置，选择能良好覆盖和泛化多个训练项目的分类器组合，确保分类器多样性；第二阶段（模块级选择）在测试时为每个新模块动态选择最胜任的分类器，实现模块级模型选择，增强对分布变化的鲁棒性。

Result: 使用4个不同CPDP基准数据集中的82个项目进行实验，结果表明该方法在大多数场景下优于现有最先进的CPDP方法。

Conclusion: 所提出的两阶段模块级模型选择框架有效缓解了跨项目分布偏移问题，通过动态适配每个模块的特性，显著提升了缺陷预测性能。

Abstract: Cross-Project Defect Prediction (CPDP) involves building models using data from external projects, called training projects, to predict modules from the target project. However, traditional CPDP methods suffer from the distribution shift between training and target projects that affects the model's performance. This paper proposes a novel CPDP framework that addresses this issue by proposing a two-stage multiple classifier system (MCS) selection scheme: one working at the project level and another at the module level. In the first stage, the framework evaluates multiple possible MCS configurations to find one that covers and generalizes well across multiple training projects. Consequently, the proposal is likely to obtain a diverse set of classifiers, each specialized in tackling software modules with distinct characteristics. The second selection stage operates at test time, selecting the most competent classifiers to predict each new module in the target project. Unlike previous approaches that apply the same classifiers to the entire target project, the proposed framework performs module-level model selection. This way, the system is more robust to changes in distributions between training and target projects because the selected set of classifiers is module-dependent. Our experimental results using 82 projects from four different CPDP benchmark datasets demonstrate that the proposed approach outperforms the state-of-the-art CPDP methods in most scenarios. The code, dataset, and further details about the proposed method are publicly available at https://github.com/jsaj/Multi_DES.

</details>


### [132] [How Developers Use Relation Chains in Gerrit-Based Review Ecosystems: An Empirical Study Across Three Open-Source Ecosystems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20189)
*Ahmed Belhouchette,Moataz Chouchen,Marouene Chaieb,Mohammad Hamdaqa Abdelwahab Hamou-Lhadj*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 该论文研究了Gerrit代码审查中"关系链"（relation chains）的采用情况及其对审查动态的影响，分析了15个仓库中的29,580条关系链，发现链式变更的合并时间比单独变更长2.6倍，审查活动在依赖链中传播，且33.5%的链成员在审查过程中发生结构演变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开发人员越来越多地通过提交一系列相关变更（而非单一大型变更）来协调依赖性的审查工作流，这种"关系链"结构在Gerrit中越来越普遍，但其对审查活动的影响尚不明确。作者旨在探究开发人员如何采用关系链，以及这些依赖结构如何影响审查动态和结果。

Method: 从三个Gerrit生态系统（OpenStack、Wikimedia、ONAP）的15个仓库中收集29,580条关系链（共401,256次变更），使用Mann-Kendall趋势检验分析链的采用趋势，Mann-Whitney检验结合Cliff's delta进行链式变更与独立变更的比较，Spearman相关分析基变更与下游变更之间的依赖关系。

Result: 关系链的普及率在5%至49%之间，且在15个仓库中有14个呈增长趋势。链式变更的中位合并时间比同等规模的独立变更长2.6倍，且对于大型变更差距更大。审查活动在依赖链中传播（基变更与下游变更的审查活动相关系数为0.43-0.61），33.5%的链成员在审查过程中经历了结构演变。

Conclusion: 关系链作为持久的、由生态系统塑造的协调单元，具有内部结构，这是以单一变更为中心的分析无法捕捉的。未来的审查分析、审阅者分配系统和AI辅助审查工具应当基于整个关系链而非孤立的变更进行推理。

Abstract: Background. Developers increasingly coordinate dependent review workflows by submitting sequences of related changes rather than monolithic ones. In Gerrit, these dependencies form relation chains: structured review units that link changes together. As chains become more common, they shape review activities through synchronization overhead, CI amplification, and merge-ordering constraints.
  Aim. We investigate how developers adopt relation chains and how these dependency structures influence review dynamics and outcomes.
  Method. We analyze 29,580 relation chains from 15 repositories across three Gerrit ecosystems (OpenStack, Wikimedia, and ONAP), comprising 401,256 changes, using Mann-Kendall trend tests, Mann-Whitney tests with Cliff's delta for chain-vs-solo comparisons, and Spearman correlations for base-descendant dependencies.
  Results. Chain prevalence ranges from 5% to 49% across projects, increasing in 14 of 15. Chain changes take a median of 2.6 times longer to merge than size-matched solo changes, with the gap widening for very large changes. Review effort propagates through dependency-linked review workflows: base-change review activity co-varies with descendant review activity (rho = 0.43-0.61 in 14-15 of 15 projects), and 33.5% of chain members undergo structural evolution during review.
  Conclusions. Relation chains operate as durable, ecosystem-shaped coordination units with internal structure that change-centric analyses cannot capture. Future review analytics, reviewer-assignment systems, and AI-assisted review tools should reason over chains rather than isolated changes.

### [133] [Don't Trust the Label: License Laundering in AI Supply Chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20300)
*James Jewitt,Hao Li,Gopi Krishnan Rajbahadur,Bram Adams,Ahmed E. Hassan*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文追踪了Hugging Face和GitHub上的232,270条数据集→模型→应用链，发现62.3%的链条中至少存在一个无声明许可证的工件，且除Permissive类许可证（95.1%存活率）外，其他义务性许可证类别的端到端存活率均低于7%，揭示了AI供应链中普遍的许可证洗钱现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管AI工件在多平台间流转时附带的许可证义务应随再分发传播，但尚无研究定量测量这些义务是否在供应链下游被保留、剥离或替换。

Method: 追踪232,270条数据集→模型→应用链，量化两种形式的许可证洗钱：无声明许可证的工件在下游获得明确标签，以及一个已声明许可证类别在再分发中被另一个替代。

Abstract: AI artifacts move through a multi-platform supply chain, spanning datasets and models on Hugging Face and applications on GitHub. While each artifact carries a license whose obligations should propagate through redistribution, no study has yet measured whether those obligations survive the chain or are stripped and replaced as artifacts move downstream. We trace 232,270 dataset$\rightarrow$model$\rightarrow$application chains and quantify two forms of license laundering: when artifacts with no declared license acquire definitive labels downstream, and when one declared license category replaces another during redistribution. We find that 62.3% of chains pass through at least one artifact with no declared license (concentrated in a small set of foundational datasets), and that every obligation-bearing license category falls below 7% end-to-end survival while the Permissive category reaches 95.1%. Based on these findings, we provide actionable recommendations for practitioners, model publishers, rights holders, and platform owners.

### [134] [Multi-Source and Cross-Scenario Strategy-Guided Code Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20353)
*Yuwei Zhao,Qianyu Xiao,Ye Cui,Yijun Yu,Yingfei Xiong*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: MoST是一种基于LLM的代码优化框架，通过跨知识源和跨场景的策略整合，解决了现有方法无法利用多源知识且策略无法跨场景迁移的问题。实验表明，MoST在多个编程语言的优化任务中显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于LLM的代码优化方法存在两个局限：(1) 策略只能来自历史提交记录，无法利用教科书、网页等其他知识源；(2) 策略只能用于原始场景（如特定编程语言），无法跨场景迁移。

Method: MoST将不同知识源的内容统一表示为证据对象，通过跨源跨场景聚类提取策略，必要时跨场景迁移生成静态分析规则。提出了自平衡加权聚类算法来平衡不同源证据对象，以及示例迁移流程保证跨场景规则质量。

Result: 在C/C++(151)、Python(150)、Rust(50)优化任务上，相比SemOpt，MoST生成的与开发者补丁完全相同或语义等价的补丁分别多出24.44%-180.00%和21.88%-37.50%。在15个真实项目上，性能测试最大提升19.72%-717.42%，平均提升4.44%-258.17%。

Conclusion: MoST通过多源知识整合和跨场景策略迁移有效提升了LLM代码优化的性能，在多个维度和场景下显著超越现有方法。

Abstract: Automated code optimization improves program performance by refactoring source code, and recent studies use LLMs to generate optimization patches. The newest approaches are strategy-guided: they summarize strategies from historical optimization commits as static analysis rules, and use these rules to match code locations for LLMs to optimize. However, these approaches have two limitations: (1) the strategies may come from other knowledge sources, such as textbooks and web pages, but the existing approaches cannot utilize them; (2) a strategy may be applicable to different scenarios, e.g., different programming languages, but existing approaches can only formalize strategies for the scenario to which the source commit belongs. To address these limitations, we propose MoST, an LLM-based code optimization framework that integrates multiple knowledge sources across scenarios. MoST uniformly represents items in different knowledge sources as evidence objects, clusters them in a cross-source and cross-scenario manner to identify strategies, and transfers them to the target scenario when necessary for generating static analysis rules. To implement this process, MoST employs a novel self-balanced weighted clustering algorithm to balance evidence objects from different knowledge sources, and a novel example transfer procedure to ensure the quality of the generated rules when transferring across scenarios. On a benchmark containing 151 C/C++, 150 Python, and 50 Rust historical optimization tasks, compared with SemOpt, MoST yields 24.44%-180.00% and 21.88%-37.50% more patches that are exactly the same as or semantically equivalent to developer patches, respectively. When optimizing 15 real-world projects, MoST achieves 19.72%-717.42% maximum improvements and 4.44%-258.17% average improvements for the performance tests in the projects, significantly outperforming SemOpt and Codex.

### [136] [SpikingMOT: A Spike-Driven Multi-Object Tracker](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19875)

TL;DR: 本文提出SpikingMOT，一种基于脉冲神经网络（SNN）的稀疏轨迹预测方法，通过激活稀疏性偏好（ASP）理论分析证明稀疏门控不劣于状态无关Dropout，在SportsMOT和DanceTrack上达到SOTA性能，同时参数减少72%，能耗降低86.7%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有MOT方法使用密集激活的人工神经网络进行运动建模，但忽略了密集响应对于轨迹预测是否必要的问题。作者希望探究如何用更稀疏、更高效的方式建模轨迹动态。

Method: 1) 理论分析激活稀疏性偏好（ASP），证明稀疏门控在相同激活率下不劣于状态无关Dropout；2) 提出SpikingMOT，将轨迹状态分解为伪轨迹基，利用当前预测误差校准后验概率进行下一帧预测，采用脉冲神经网络实现稀疏自适应建模。

Result: SportsMOT上HOTA 74.9，DanceTrack上HOTA 56.5，参数减少72%，能耗降低86.7%，达到SOTA。

Abstract: Multi-object tracking (MOT) plays a fundamental role in visual perception, where accurate trajectory prediction is essential for reliable target association under complex motion patterns. Recent trackers have improved motion modeling with densely activated artificial neural networks, yet they largely overlook whether such dense responses are necessary for trajectory prediction. In this paper, we formulate activation sparsity preference (ASP) by tackling two key questions: 1. How can we identify a model architecture that appropriately and formally explains ASP, and 2. How can we translate this explanation into competitive tracking performance. Theoretical analysis shows that sparse gating is no worse than state-independent dropout under the same activation rate. Based on this insight, SpikingMOT is proposed as a spike-driven tracker that adaptively models sparse trajectory dynamics with spiking neural networks (SNNs). Specifically, SpikingMOT decomposes each trajectory state into pseudo-trajectory bases and uses the current prediction error to calibrate the posterior for next-frame prediction. With this brain-inspired loop, SpikingMOT achieves state-of-the-art performance in extensive experiments, 74.9 HOTA on SportsMOT and 56.5 HOTA on DanceTrack, while reducing the parameters and energy by 72% and 86.7%, respectively. These results bring SNNs into MOT, opening a promising direction for efficient tracking.

### [137] [Native Multi-Dimensional Subquadratic Operators via Input Dependent Long Convolutions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19378)
*David R. Wessels,Farhad Ramezanghorbani,David W. Romero,Alireza Moradzadeh,Olivia Viessmann,Maksim Zhdanov,John St. John,Ken Janik,David M Knigge,Yucheng Tang,Erik J Bekkers,Saee Gopal Paliwal*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: HyenaND是一种亚二次、全局、输入依赖的算子，可直接作用于多维数据的原生几何结构，通过隐式参数化的全局、输入依赖的多维卷积核实现，并在多种长上下文任务中匹配或超越注意力基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有亚二次注意力替代方案在处理多维数据时存在局限：标准卷积缺乏全局感受野和输入依赖性，循环模型需要将图像、体积和PDE等多维数据光栅化为违反空间结构的1D扫描顺序。

Method: 提出HyenaND算子，通过隐式参数化的全局、输入依赖的多维卷积核直接作用于多维数据的原生几何结构；开发CUDA实现nSubQ，融合FFT-卷积路径以实现O(L log L)缩放的理论加速。

Result: 纯HyenaND堆叠在长上下文基因组学、计算机视觉、医学成像和PDE建模中匹配强注意力基线的精度；混合配置（HyenaND与注意力层交错）则超越纯注意力和基于循环的强混合模型。

Conclusion: HyenaND在无需妥协数据几何结构的前提下，实现了亚二次复杂度与全局输入依赖性的兼顾，验证了纯亚二次算子在实际任务中的竞争力，且与注意力结合能进一步提升性能。

Abstract: Subquadratic alternatives to attention require compromises when applied to multi-dimensional data: standard convolutions lack global receptive fields and input dependency, while recurrent models require rasterizing data such as images, volumes, and partial differential equation (PDE) into an ad-hoc $1\rm D$ scan order that violates their spatial structure. We introduce \textit{HyenaND}, a subquadratic, global, input-dependent operator that acts directly on the native geometry of multidimensional data through convolutions with implicitly parametrized global, input-dependent multi-dimensional convolutional kernels. Our CUDA implementation, \texttt{nSubQ}, fuses the FFT-convolution path to turn HyenaND's $\mathcal{O}(L \log L)$ scaling into wall-clock speedups. Across long-context genomics, computer vision, medical imaging, and PDE modeling, pure HyenaND stacks match the accuracy of strong attention baselines, while hybrid configurations that interleave HyenaND and attention layers outperform both pure attention and strong recurrence-based hybrids.

### [138] [Bayesian Wind Tunnels for Model Selection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19379)
*Siddhartha R Dalal,Vishal Misra,Abhay Parekh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了Transformer能否进行贝叶斯模型选择（即从数据中识别正确的假设类别）。通过构建“模型选择贝叶斯风洞”环境，发现2.8M参数的Transformer能在固定点自由对合任务中达到接近贝叶斯最优的熵一致性（0.01-bit），并能进行非嵌套类比较。关键发现是：当判别统计量需要算术运算时，模型选择在整数token下成功，但在不透明符号下完全失败，且该边界在112倍参数扩展后依然存在。对前沿LLM的探测显示其具有定性贝叶斯行为但校准差距很大（~55x）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究表明Transformer能在固定假设类别内进行精确贝叶斯滤波，但尚不清楚它们是否能进行贝叶斯模型选择——即从数据中识别出正确的假设类别。本文旨在填补这一空白，探究Transformer能否超越简单的假设类内推理，进行跨类别的模型选择。

Method: 设计模型选择贝叶斯风洞环境，提供封闭形式的真实后验概率。使用固定点自由对合（f(f(x))=x）作为主要测试任务，配合3-cycles等非嵌套比较任务。系统性地操纵感知访问条件（整数token vs. 不透明符号），测试算术操作（模加、模乘）的影响，并进行参数扩展实验（2.8M到316M）和站定性控制实验。

Result: 2.8M参数Transformer在固定点自由对合任务中达到0.01-bit熵一致性；非嵌套比较（对合vs.3-cycles）的类后验MAE低于0.001；算术任务中整数token成功但符号token完全失败，该边界在112倍参数扩展后依然存在；站定性控制（固定重标号）下符号token成功；故障定位在头部反转与算术的组合而非头部解析本身；前沿LLM显示~55x校准差距。

Conclusion: Transformer确实具备贝叶斯模型选择能力，但存在关键的感知访问条件：当需要算术推理时，模型严重依赖token的稳定语义（如数字），无法仅凭不透明符号关系进行有效的电路编译。这一局限性在参数大幅扩展后依然存在，表明它可能是Transformer架构的固有约束，而非规模问题。此外，即使是大规模LLM在贝叶斯校准上也远非完美。

Abstract: Prior work has shown that transformers can perform exact Bayesian filtering within a fixed
  hypothesis class. Can they also perform Bayesian model selection -- identifying the correct
  hypothesis class from data? We introduce model-selection Bayesian wind tunnels: controlled
  environments where ground-truth posteriors over hypothesis classes are available in closed
  form. Using fixed-point-free involutions -- whose defining property f(f(x))=x is purely
  relational -- a 2.8M-parameter transformer achieves 0.01-bit entropy agreement with the
  Bayesian optimum (3 seeds), with both integer tokens and opaque symbols whose meanings
  change every episode. This extends to non-nested comparisons: involutions vs. 3-cycles
  (where neither class is a subset of the other) achieve class-posterior MAE under 0.001,
  demonstrating genuine model selection beyond simplicity/subset bias. We then identify a
  sharp perceptual access condition: when the discriminative statistic requires arithmetic --
  modular addition (rotations) or multiplication (f(x)=cx mod p) -- model selection succeeds
  with integer tokens but fails completely with opaque symbols, and this boundary persists
  under 112x scaling (2.8M to 316M parameters). A stationarity control confirms the operative
  factor: opaque tokens with a fixed relabeling succeed (0.009-bit MAE), showing that stable
  semantics, not integer identity, enable circuit compilation. Header subtask diagnostics
  localize the failure to the composition of header inversion with arithmetic rather than
  header parsing itself. Probing frontier LLMs on the same tasks shows qualitative Bayesian
  behavior but a large calibration gap (~55x), measured through lossy probes and therefore
  directional rather than exact.

</details>


### [139] [CruiseBench: A Real-Flight-Aligned N-CMAPSS Benchmark for Engine RUL Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19380)
*Pu Cheng,Qiang Miao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出CruiseBench，一个从N-CMAPSS数据集中提取巡航阶段的RUL预测基准，通过CPM-N-CMAPSS掩码工具实现阶段筛选，并给出多模型基线结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: N-CMAPSS数据集虽然更真实，但全飞行记录数据量大且退化信号与工况变化混杂，导致预处理选择和RUL建模性能的直接比较变得复杂困难。

Method: 提出CPM-N-CMAPSS掩码工具识别巡航阶段；制定固定协议：仅用场景描述符和实测传感器，排除虚拟传感器等；保留原生分辨率窗口；应用数据集级RUL上限。

Result: 在CruiseBench-eta5-W256-S10设置下，TSMixer取得最低平均RMSE（3.4±1.71）和Saxena得分（(2.50±2.99)×10⁴）。消融实验表明飞行阶段选择、时间下采样方法和RUL上限阈值影响结果。

Conclusion: CruiseBench提供可控、可复现的RUL模型比较基准；CPM-N-CMAPSS为迁移学习和域适应研究提供阶段特定的数据基础。

Abstract: Remaining useful life (RUL) prediction estimates how long an engine can continue safe operation and is central to maintenance planning. N-CMAPSS extends C-MAPSS by simulating run-to-failure aero-engine trajectories using recorded real-flight profiles and retaining complete within-flight time series rather than cycle-level snapshots. However, this added realism reduces evaluation control because full-flight records increase data volume and entangle degradation cues with operating-regime variation, complicating preprocessing choices and direct comparisons of RUL modeling performance. To mitigate this issue, this paper proposes CruiseBench, a cruise-stage RUL benchmark derived from N-CMAPSS. It introduces CPM-N-CMAPSS (Cruising-Period Mask for N-CMAPSS), a mask artifact that stores cycle-local cruising intervals identified by the common-altitude method for the nine accessible subdatasets. CruiseBench applies a fixed protocol to the masked rows, using scenario descriptors and measured sensors as inputs while excluding virtual sensors, health parameters, and auxiliary metadata from the feature tensor, preserving native-resolution windows, and applying dataset-wise RUL caps. Experiments with LSTM, GRU, TCN, and TSMixer provide baseline results for this setting. Under CruiseBench-eta5-W256-S10, TSMixer obtains the lowest average RMSE, $3.4\pm1.71$, and Saxena score, $(2.50\pm2.99)\times 10^{4}$. Ablation studies show that flight-stage selection, temporal downscaling method, and RUL-cap threshold affect reported results. With its fixed cruise-stage protocol, CruiseBench provides a reproducible sub-benchmark for controlled RUL model comparison and CPM-N-CMAPSS provides a stage-specific data foundation for future transfer-learning and domain-adaptation studies.

### [142] [SUM: Unified Geometric Surgery on Spatio-Temporal Adaptation Vectors for Federated Class Incremental Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19384)
*Jaeik Kim,Jaeyoung Do*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出SUM框架，将联邦类增量学习(FCIL)重新解释为统一的多任务学习问题，通过对服务器端聚合过程中的时空自适应向量进行几何手术，在不增加客户端计算、通信或存储开销的情况下，有效缓解了时空灾难性遗忘问题，在多个视觉和语言基准上相比现有方法提升高达22%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有FCIL方法通常用分离的机制处理空间干扰（异构客户端）和时间干扰（序列任务），导致客户端计算或通信开销增加，且未规范聚合过程中更新之间的方向性交互，从而引发时空灾难性遗忘(ST-CF)。

Method: 将FCIL重新定义为统一的多任务学习问题，将客户端和任务更新表示为共享参数空间中的自适应向量；提出SUM框架，在服务器端对时空自适应向量进行几何手术：空间SUM缓解每轮内的客户端级干扰，因果在线时序SUM随时间消除跨任务干扰，且无需额外的客户端计算、通信或存储。

Result: 在多种视觉和语言基准上，SUM相比现有FCIL方法提升高达22%，同时对不可靠客户端保持鲁棒性，且计算效率高。

Conclusion: 通过统一视角和纯服务器端操作，SUM有效解决了FCIL中的时空干扰耦合问题，为分布式持续学习提供了一种高效、鲁棒的解决方案。

Abstract: Real-world intelligent systems often require both distributed collaboration across data-isolated clients and continual adaptation to evolving tasks. This setting naturally gives rise to Federated Class Incremental Learning (FCIL), which combines Federated Learning (FL) and Continual Learning (CL). However, their combination introduces two coupled sources of interference: spatial interference from heterogeneous clients and temporal interference from sequential tasks, jointly leading to Spatial-Temporal Catastrophic Forgetting (ST-CF). Existing approaches typically address spatial and temporal interference with separate mechanisms, often incurring additional client-side computation or communication, while leaving directional interactions among updates during aggregation unregulated. In this paper, we reinterpret FCIL as a unified multi-task learning problem, where both client and task updates are represented as adaptation vectors in a shared parameter space. Based on this view, we propose Unified Geometric Surgery on Spatio-Temporal Adaptation Vectors (SUM), a purely server-side framework that performs geometric surgery on adaptation vectors during aggregation. Spatial SUM mitigates client-level interference within each round, while causal online temporal SUM removes cross-task interference over time without additional client-side computation, communication, or memory beyond standard federated training. Empirically, SUM achieves up to 22% improvement over prior FCIL methods across diverse vision and language benchmarks while remaining robust to unreliable clients and maintaining computational efficiency.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究依赖自动可解释性分数（autointerpretability scores）进行SAE的跨论文比较，但该方法假设分数反映的是特征本身的稳定性质而非评估管线中的混淆因素。作者质疑这一假设是否成立。

Method: 在四种指标（simulation, detection, fuzzing, purity）、两个模型（Pythia-160M, Apertus-8B）和四个方法论变化轴上进行系统实验，分析评估管线中各因素对分数的影响。

Result: 发现：(R1)方法论方差在所有指标和模型上均超过架构方差；(R2)各指标稳定性曲线不同，detection最稳定，fuzzing最不可靠；(R3)top-k特征排序在不同语料和draw条件下不一致，均值稳定的背后是单个特征层面的不稳定。

Conclusion: 跨论文比较可能反映的是管线差异而非架构差异，这对SAE有效性的争论有重要影响。作者提供了方差分解方法、稳定性检查工具和最低报告清单以改进评估。

Abstract: Cross-paper comparison of sparse autoencoder (SAE) interpretability often relies on autointerpretability scores. In this evaluation pipeline, a language model (LM) explains each feature, and another LM scores the explanation. For these comparisons to be meaningful, scores must reflect stable properties of the features rather than confounding aspects of the evaluation pipeline. Through systematic experiments across four metrics (simulation, detection, fuzzing, purity), two models (Pythia-160M, Apertus-8B), and four axes of methodological variation, we show that this assumption does not hold. Specifically, we find that R1) methodological variance collectively exceeds architectural variance across all metrics and tested models; R2) each metric exhibits a distinct instability profile, with detection being the most stable and fuzzing unreliable across all conditions; R3) top-k feature rankings do not stay consistent across corpus and draw conditions, masking per-feature instability behind stable mean scores; a failure that cannot be detected by monitoring explanation similarity alone. These findings suggest that cross-paper comparisons based on autointerpretability scores may reflect pipeline differences rather than architectural differences, with implications for the ongoing debate on SAE utility. More broadly, unreliable evaluation slows progress in interpretability research at a time when reliable tools for understanding AI systems are needed. To support evaluation, we contribute a variance decomposition approach, a Stability Check, and a Minimum Reporting Checklist.

### [145] [Scale-Aware Learning of Chaotic Dynamics on Unstructured Meshes via Binned Spectral Losses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19387)
*Kanad Sen,Romit Maulik*

TL;DR: 本文针对非结构网格上的高维非线性动力系统代理建模，提出将傅里叶频带功率损失扩展为图拉普拉斯频带损失，并设计了可扩展的切比雪夫多项式滤波器和多层级GLEAM方法，在湍流预测中显著提升了长时间滚动的保真度和统计不变量的保持能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
